Free Talk

Random Jottings

Savior of Marital Discord 211

— Zhanlu

For couples who are at each other's throats, there is no need to appoint a lawyer or declare a separation. Just invite two saviors, and they can be as loving as ever, transforming fighting chickens into lovebirds.

Who are these saviors? Not Sha Wujing, but Duidui.

What is Sha Wujing? Sha Wujing is also known as sand grubs. It is a type of caterpillar that can spin soil to create tunnels, creating an ant's hell, causing ants to fall into it and be devoured. It likes to sleep and is also called the "sleeping worm." If someone catches it and places it in the couple's pillow, it can harmonize their feelings. Chen Cangqi's "Materia Medica," "Jianhu Ji," and "Changtan Suilu" all say this. Therefore, Sha Wujing is the savior of marital discord.

What is Duidui? Duidui is also the name of an insect, shaped like a tick. It always travels in pairs, male and female, like a loving couple walking arm in arm. It is found in Yunnan, Myanmar, and other places. If someone catches it and sells it to wealthy families, it can often fetch a high price. It is then placed in a silver box and placed in the couple's pillow, ensuring eternal harmony and no chance of turning against each other. "Youhuan Yutan" and Zhan Jingfeng's "Xiaobian" both say this. Therefore, Duidui is the savior of marital discord.

Can these insignificant insects really be the saviors of marital discord? We will not know without trying. I advise discordant couples: even after taking a hundred steps together, there is still hesitation. How much more when sharing the same bed, pillow, quilt, and covers? If everyone can think like this, the savior is within reach, and there is no need to seek help from small insects.

Spiritual Civilization 212

— Yiweisheng

Fellow countrymen, listen!

The idea of spiritual civilization has indeed harmed us quite a bit. Because of the concept of valuing the spirit and despising material things, we resort to spiritual civilization to resolve all kinds of unbearable situations. For example, some bad people are given names like jackals, tigers, leopards, poisonous snakes, and fierce beasts. These are merely metaphors for their wickedness and do not mean that they are actually these things. However, many people who have suffered at the hands of these wicked people do not have the courage to resist or retaliate. Instead, they secretly use the idea of spiritual civilization to comfort themselves, saying: "He is not a human, he is a beast, a poisonous snake. I am a human. Why should a human bicker with beasts and poisonous snakes?" With this thought of spiritual civilization, everything comes to an end. They endure all kinds of shame and tolerate all kinds of violations. From individuals to families to nations, they all use this idea of spiritual civilization to restrain themselves. Who knows that the person who insults you is still actually a human being and will never actually turn into a real snake or beast just because of your spiritual thought? You don't want to argue with him? He insists on arguing with you. He doesn't have to worry about turning into a snake or beast, but you yourself may become a cow, horse, or slave. Furthermore, even if it is a real snake or beast, if it comes to attack us, can we not respond? In my opinion, only children who are full of vigor and vitality do not understand what spiritual civilization is and have not been poisoned by spiritual civilization.

The Philosophy of Giving Up Seats 213

— Jingbo

The Difference Between Young Women and Old Women

"Ladies first!" Why? Because women are weaker than men. Also, pregnant women and those carrying children may feel various inconveniences when walking, riding in vehicles, and in other public places. Therefore, men should give way to them out of a natural compassion and moral concept. When crowded, let them go first. In dangerous situations, let them escape first. In vehicles, let them sit down first. This is the moral expression that should be present in social life and the instinct of biological group protection. It originally does not involve the mixing of vanity and requests, nor does it look down on women as weak and incompetent. However, on streetcars, we often see that beautiful young women easily get people to give up their seats, while ragged old women can only stand!

Logically speaking, no matter what kind of young woman she is, if another old woman gets on a public tram or bus and cannot find a seat and is standing in front of you, and at this time, you and your friend happen to have two seats that you can give to them, you should of course stand up together and let them both sit. If there is only one seat, you should let the old woman sit first because she is the weaker of the women. The principle is very simple. However, because there is the gaze of beautiful eyes, the reward of a smile, and the request of a soul-stirring "thank you" or "excuse me," just like roads are specially designed for cars, giving up seats is almost exclusively for beautiful young women.

To reiterate: if a young woman is not beautiful, she is considered by most passengers giving up their seats to be the same as an old woman who can be ignored. In addition to not having the aforementioned requests, there is also the psychology of "no need to give up the seat."

The major revelation is: is the starting point of moral behavior between the concepts of "self-interest" and "class"?

The Wonders of Advertising Techniques 214

— Xu Wanhua

A Good Textbook on Advertising

The great and miraculous power of advertising to attract business is almost unbelievable. In the past decade, our countrymen have come to pay attention to it, engaging in intense competition and rivalry to gain an advantage in newspapers. They understand that casting bait to catch fish requires only a small amount of promotional expenses to reap profits a hundred or a thousand times greater.

However, how can advertising text be made captivating? It requires ingenuity, discernible only by a clever and skillful mind. If we peruse foreign newspapers, we can see that their advertisements transform the mundane into the extraordinary, demonstrating that foreign advertising has kept pace with scientific development and entered a path of prosperity. Compared to the mindless "big discount," "big sale," "adding three inches to the foot," and "matching codes for half price" advertisements common in our country, they are worlds apart. I now record several instances of ingenious foreign advertisements as models for our countrymen to improve their designs.

In England, a general merchandise store one day published an advertisement in a daily newspaper, titled "New Marriage Method." The method involved dividing the store's merchandise into two categories, one sold only to men and the other only to women, each with numbered items, up to a certain number of tens of thousands. A particular number was designated as the lottery prize. Once all the items were sold, the store would identify the man and woman who both possessed the winning lottery number and introduce them to each other, arranging for them to become husband and wife, with a large dowry provided as a gift. If no match could be found, the dowry would be divided between the two parties. This attracted shoppers from far and wide. After the numbers were exhausted, the dowry was divided because the man and woman were not of suitable age. After three such attempts, a man and woman finally matched and married, and the store made countless profits.

Another store, seeing this and envying it, also published an advertisement, saying: "Our store has a daughter, just of marriageable age, with unparalleled beauty, seeking a good match. Anyone interested in seeking a partner is invited to come to the store for a meeting to facilitate selection." People rushed to the store. Indeed, there was a woman standing at the entrance, shaking hands with each guest as a greeting. Back and forth they came, wearing out the threshold, but those who came could not simply leave after a quick look, so they mostly lingered for a while buying things. The store's profits increased a hundredfold. After more than a year, they published another advertisement, saying: "The woman has met many people, but few have pleased her. The search for a partner is now concluded."

A man, heartbroken from a failed romance, committed suicide in despair. A gun store, hearing of this, quickly sought out a scenic spot with beautiful landscapes of water and trees, and erected a white stone tombstone, boldly inscribed: "[Mr. So-and-so, who committed suicide with the latest model pistol from our store]." The inscription then detailed the incident. Tourists passing by could not help but notice it, and the store's name became widely known, leading to a thriving business.

Praying for Rain by Kowtowing 215

— Qian

President Sun Eats a Little Hardship, the County Magistrate Bravely Proclaims Action

Last summer, we suffered from floods; this summer, we suffer from drought. Amidst the cries of drought, I received a letter from my younger sister at home, which I transcribe below:

[Brother Qian:

...I am now telling you about a recent event.

X County, because of the prolonged lack of rain and the prevalence of epidemics, everyone thought of a proper way to avoid it. This method was jointly planned by the county magistrate and the people of the entire county. What is this method? I'm afraid you can't even imagine it. It turned out that they initiated an [association] that stipulated that all the people of the county must burn incense and eat vegetarian food, the city gates were closed for three days, and the county magistrate himself would bathe and purify himself every day, going to the four city gates to kowtow and pray for rain, and move the City God Bodhisattva out for a procession through the four gates, with the county magistrate leading the rear. That's already bad enough, but the most hateful thing is that our President Sun's portrait was also carried behind the City God Bodhisattva, parading around the city. In the period of political tutelage, they actually came up with such a gimmick! I grieve for China! President Sun's principles have not been implemented, but he has already been treated as an [idol]!...]

There are many more emotional words, which I will not record now. As for X County, located on the edge of X Lake in Anhui Province, it should not be subject to drought. However, water conservancy is not developed, rivers are not dredged, the mountains are bare, and there is no cultivation of forests. The county magistrate and party officials probably couldn't even dream of so-called scientific knowledge. How can there not be drought?

Silver Threads 217

— Jiang Hongjiao

Mr. Wang also lived in this town, only a street away from Yuan Fenruo's residence. He was already fifty-six years old, and also a widower. His children had all died, and he often felt the loneliness of being a widower. Sometimes when he caught a cold and coughed, or when his back ached and he couldn't get out of bed, he especially felt isolated. He recalled the pleasures of family life in the past, and occasionally still felt sexual frustration. He had a strong desire to find a suitable woman as a companion in his old age. But he was very poor, and his age was too far past the marrying age. He was very disappointed, knowing that no woman would be willing to marry him as a wife.

But he was very fond of Yu Fenruo, and he couldn't think of any way to find out if she was willing to remarry, or if she was willing to marry a poor old man. Every time he went to her house to distribute or collect embroidery, he carefully observed everything about her. He felt that although she was a woman in her forties, only wearing plain cloth clothes, her face didn't seem to have completely aged away the charming beauty of her youth. Her house didn't have any good furniture, but it was tidy and clean. She treated the irrelevant madman very kindly and considerately, and her heart was very good. Everything met the conditions that Mr. Wang wanted for marrying a remarried woman, but the wages she earned from embroidery were enough to support herself and also to take care of Yuan the madman's life. She was very dignified, her life wasn't in a panic, and she lived her days very steadily, not needing to remarry. Mr. Wang had tried several times to miscalculate her wages and give her two jiao extra, but she was also very good at arithmetic and returned the overpayment to Mr. Wang. Sometimes he bought some soap, towels, and white sugar and sent them to her, but she only slightly accepted a portion, but she bought things of equal value and sent them back to Mr. Wang; and declared to Mr. Wang, please don't send things again, otherwise she would be unable to reciprocate, and could only decline everything. Mr. Wang's wish couldn't be achieved, but he didn't hate her because of this, but instead respected her very much.

Yu Fenruo's kindness was known to everyone; Yuan the madman's madness was hated by the whole town. When Yuan the madman was crazy, he would slap people for no reason, curse young women to become widows, or scold young girls for having affairs, or strongly pull the police to talk about her husband, so everyone hated him, was angry at him, and wanted to beat him; but Yu Fenruo knew, and would definitely go to plead and apologize for him. When people heard Yu Fenruo's words, they would calm down and nothing would happen. The police station repeatedly wanted to arrest him and send him to an insane asylum, but Fenruo would always persuade them to stop. When Yuan the madman was crazy, Fenruo often told him about his madness, and he knew that he had offended many people when he was crazy. He was very grateful that Fenruo was taking care of him like this, otherwise he might have been beaten to death, or captured and taken to the insane asylum.

Silver Dollar Market Enters a Better State 221

▲Market Sentiment Turns and the Situation Frequently Improves Financial circles are unwilling to rashly release loans for any needs amidst the current commercial recession. Therefore, since the resumption of business after the first half of the year, everything has been generally contracted, and the situation has been lifeless. For more than half a year, there has been no good news to record. According to people in the industry, after this September, various industries seem to have hopes for development, and the need for silver dollar transactions can also be slowly activated. The market is expected to turn around, so yesterday, the silver and dollar markets both generally improved.

▲The Discount Rises and Borrowing Rates Increase by Four Points [Dollar Discount] The early market saw an improvement in the discount rate as the market turned for the better, calculated at six mace, eight fen, nine li, one hao, two hu, and a half, an increase of two hao and a half compared to the previous afternoon. The afternoon market continued to rise by eight hao and seven hu and a half, to six mace and nine fen. As a result, the total increase between the two markets was slightly more than one li. [Silver Borrowing Rate] Also turned better yesterday. Both the morning and afternoon markets were at eight fen, a sudden improvement of four points compared to the previous day, with the addition of water also reaching a market price of eight or nine fen. The silver market situation is quite strong.

▲Copper Coins Frequently Discover New Prices The Jiangnan small dollar trend is stable. Yesterday, it only rose by half a li, calculated at five mace, nine fen, six li, and a half, mostly comparable to the past. There was no significant difference between the morning and afternoon markets on this day, with 6,000 corners traded in the morning market and 3,000 corners in the afternoon market. The Guangdong small dollar fell in the early market to five mace, eight fen, one li, two hao, and a half, and remained at the original level in the afternoon market, at five mace, eight fen, two li. The trading volume was 145,000 corners in the morning market and 55,000 corners in the afternoon market. Copper coins, due to the influx of supply-side supports, gradually increased, adding another 1,000 wen yesterday, to 434,000 wen, opening a new high price. The trading volume was 56,420 strings, calculated at a silver price of 13,000 taels.

▲Silver Remittances are Appropriately Simple and Complex Yesterday's bank remittances seemed inferior to the previous day, and the settlement replenishment was still around two to three million. Warehousing was one million three hundred thousand, silver pawn transactions were over ninety thousand, and money house silver public single remittances were thirty-one million one hundred thousand. Silver overdraft remittances were over four million one hundred thousand, liquor remittances from various roads were over eighty thousand, and cash withdrawals were over one million.

Grain and Rice Market Affected by Rainfall 226

▲South Shanghai: Yesterday, due to continuous rain, the sources of supply from various guilds were scarce. At the morning opening, the prices of new japonica rice and Zhongguan white rice increased by twenty cents. The price of fresh northern japonica rice was fixed, and the opening of rice from ships will have to wait for the weather to clear.

▲New Docks: About a dozen rice boats from Changshu and Xishan, carrying rice etc., arrived. Yesterday, at 4:30 PM, a survey showed that there were more than 250 rice boats near Hengfeng Bridge and Laji Bridge, each carrying about 80 dan (a unit of weight). The total amount was estimated to be around 20,000 dan. Affected by the rain, the rice on the boats could not be opened for sale. The prices of thin rice, northern japonica rice, and new japonica rice each rose by ten to twenty cents.

Imported Rice Market Turns Stable 227

The Local Appetite Remains Good

Extension of Deadline for Reporting Transit Shipments Until the End of the Year

Yesterday, the appetite of imported rice merchants was sluggish. Merchants from distant regions were uniformly cautious. Some local households recently had wholesalers allocating goods, and their appetite was satisfied, but not enthusiastically. The entire market only saw small transactions of two small cars of rice going to Changzhou and other places inland. There were no other transactions. However, the appetite of the Japanese community remained active, and there were continuous engagements. Yesterday, the prices of white rice were high, and the intention to purchase was more active. A total of 1,500 to 1,600 bags of Saigon rice were purchased, with prices ranging from 8.80 to 8.70 yuan per bag. 1,500 bags of No. 1 Saigon rice were sold, with prices ranging from 9.50 to 9.30 yuan. No other rice was sold.

Furthermore, it is reported that according to custom, after imported rice arrives, it must be reported to customs within a certain period. After reporting, the goods can only be picked up in this city and cannot be re-exported. Currently, customs will strictly impose fines to urge cargo owners to report. Yesterday, the Rice and Grain Trade Association requested the Customs Administration to extend the implementation deadline. It is said that the Customs Administration has agreed to extend the deadline to the end of the year.

Flour Market in a Slump 229

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the prices for all months turned flat and sluggish again. Quoted prices for imported wheat have fallen by about five to six or seven jiao for two consecutive days. Foreigners' confidence naturally turned quiet again. However, the major factories remained on the sidelines, without any action. Therefore, although market sentiment was not good, the decline was not too drastic. The smaller factories made slight sales, but the amount was insignificant. According to the current situation, the quoted price of imported wheat is the key factor. The actual sales in the domestic market are not given much attention. As a result, the closing price for this month was one fen lower than the previous month, October was one fen and two and a half li lower, November was one fen and a half lower, December was one fen and two and a half li lower, January was five li lower, and the opening price for February was 1 liang and 9 qian and 7 fen, with a better closing price of five li.

Futures Wheat Falls Six to Seven Fen 230

Yesterday, after the opening of the futures wheat market in the morning and afternoon, prices for all months generally trended downward again. Quoted prices for imported wheat have fallen by five, six, or seven jiao for two consecutive days. Therefore, most clients considered selling back, and the opening market price was small. The factories were generally lukewarm because the prices were not cost-effective. It is estimated that there will be no intention to purchase until the price reaches the 5 qian and 1 guan level. Therefore, the future market trend is unlikely to be optimistic. As a result, September fell seven fen, October fell six fen, November fell five fen, and January fell six fen. Spot wheat has not yet opened for trading because the delivery period has just passed.

Demand for Raw Silk Cocoons in Wuxi Exceeds Supply 232

Top-Grade Spring Cocoons Eagerly Purchased Without Remainder

Medium and Lower-Grade Goods Will Also Be Sold Out

Wuxi has always been a well-known cocoon-producing area. This year, both spring and summer cocoons experienced poor harvests. Moreover, after the spring cocoons entered the market, the sales of European and American silk declined, and financial conditions were tight. No one inquired about the new cocoons. Cocoon merchants generally transported their stored cocoons to Shanghai for sale or as collateral for loans. As a result, the inventory of cocoons in Wuxi was insufficient. In the middle of last month, silk sales by foreign firms suddenly became brisk. Silk factories started purchasing raw materials, and they bid up prices for European cocoons of superior foreign varieties. The price rose several times a day. In the middle of last month, the total volume of dry cocoon transactions reached several thousand dan. The top-grade goods have all been eagerly purchased without remainder, and the medium and lower-grade goods will also be sold out. Supply cannot meet demand. If there is no hope for a bumper autumn cocoon harvest, a cocoon shortage is bound to occur. Currently, the price of slow cocoons has risen to over 200 yuan.

Yellow and White Raw Silk Increasingly Popular 233

Yesterday, the raw silk market in the foreign firms in this city became increasingly popular. European and American firms showed a stronger appetite for yellow and white raw silk. Due to the lack of raw materials and the scarcity of stored silk, market sentiment became increasingly popular. Yesterday, Xinfu and other firms imported 60 bales of superior-grade AB-grade 13-15 denier Shanghai white factory silk at prices ranging from 680 to 740 taels. Ganli imported 120 bales of Lingma brand top-grade No. 2 Qili white dry silk at a price of 625 taels. Dachang imported 40 bales of medium-grade 13-15 denier Fenlu yellow factory silk at a price of 600 taels.

Tunxi Special Green Tea Sales to England Show Slight Movement 234

Yesterday, the English firms Jinlong, Xiehe, Yihua, and others, as well as the China Tea Company, which handle special green teas from Tunxi, Xiuning, and Wudong, showed a slight increase in appetite due to receiving reply telegrams from Morocco. A total of over ten zi (a unit of measure) were shipped throughout the city. The selling price did not change much. The market for Wubei Gongse special green tea remained stagnant. There were only scattered transactions of needle tea, show tea, and Gongxi tea. There was no major progress in the situation.

Demand for Piece Goods and Woolens from Sichuan and Jiangxi Guilds is Strong 235

Yesterday, the Jiangxi and Sichuan guilds showed a strong appetite for woolens and wool goods. There were considerable transactions in items such as plaid, plain, mixed-color, and iridescent Walter wool, common evergreen gray mixed-color serge, diagonal dot covert cloth, suit wool, plain thick Melford cloth, and three-four ounce frame overcoat wool, and wide and narrow striped camel hair, and the trading was very lively. Boxes were sent by parcel post through the post office.

Large Metal Ingots of Lead Surge by Over One Liang 236

Yesterday, the metal market still felt flat. Although there were some small sales to customers, the amount was not large. Apart from necessary items, factories and construction guilds did not inquire about or purchase large quantities. However, the lead business was more lively than others yesterday due to considerable absorption by hoarding merchants. The details of the main items are recorded separately below:

▲Fixed Prices for Large Lead Ingots Soar: Yesterday, overseas telegrams indicated that large lead ingots were priced at 45 gold yuan per ton, a continuous increase of more than 5 gold yuan compared to the previous day. The market sentiment in this city was temporarily good, and the market atmosphere became stronger. Therefore, the standard price rose from 11 liang and 2.5 qian to 11 liang and 7.5 qian. Yesterday afternoon, the asking price even reached 12 liang and 5 qian. Although actual customers had not yet opened, transactions had already occurred at the market prices of 12 liang and 12 liang and 1 or 2 qian (mostly purchased by hoarding merchants). Therefore, the sharp trend in the market was unmatched by other metal products. The standard price of Hunan native lead, which had been rarely inquired about for a long time, also jumped significantly yesterday. The lowest price on the market was only 10 liang and 2.5 qian per dan, but yesterday the asking price also frequently increased to 12 liang. It was reported that 700 to 800 bars were offered on the market at 11 liang and 2 or 3 qian, which were purchased by fellow traders. The market price of 12 liang had not actually opened, but judging from the recent market sentiment, this estimate is likely to be realized soon.

▲Inventory of Galvanized Iron Sheets Depleted: Recently, the remaining inventory of galvanized iron sheets has been selling less and less. Therefore, the market trend has evolved into a situation where supply cannot meet demand. The standard price has been increasing steadily. Currently, the market price for 22-gauge is estimated at 9 liang per dan, 24-gauge at 9 liang and 5 qian, 26-gauge at 11 liang and 2.5 qian, and 28-gauge at 11 liang and 5 qian, all increasing by several qian compared to the previous market price.

▲Thin Galvanized Iron Sheets Declining: The market for thin British galvanized iron sheets has recently declined significantly, while inventories are abundant, causing panic in the market. The market price is trending downward. It is estimated that the price per sheet is 9 qian and 6 fen for 7 feet, 9 qian and 3 fen for the second grade, and 8 qian for 6 feet and 7 qian and 7 fen for the second grade. It is reported that only 3,000 to 4,000 sheets have been sold in recent days.

Sugar Market Sees Rise in Raw Sugar and White Sugar 237

Yesterday, the Shanghai Sugar Exchange market remained quiet. The atmospheric pressure for No. 24 Dutch raw sugar was slightly stronger, and the transaction price rose to 14 liang and 3 qian. Although there were not many transactions, the market was quite firm. Transactions of fine granulated white sugar at 14 liang and 3 qian and 7.5 fen were still brisk. The market for No. 8 and 9 Dutch red sugar remained the same, with very few transactions. Tai Koo Sugar B at 6 liang and 1.5 qian, CW mark at 15 liang and 6.5 qian, HX mark at 15 liang, H mark at 12 liang and 3 qian all saw quiet demand. PX sugar at 11 liang and 2.5 qian was quite popular, and the market has been reported as exhausted. Although the sale of Dutch sugar has gradually become active, the foreign firms Tianxiang and Dachang, which are selling off original raw sugar, have little hope of a transaction at this time because of the lack of strong intention to purchase from the trading houses.

Coal Market Sees Sluggish Transactions Due to Rain 238

Yesterday, transactions for various types of coal were sluggish due to rain. Sales of white coal were even weaker, and market prices softened slightly. Shanxi coal blocks sold for 15 liang yesterday, a decrease of 2 qian and 5 fen compared to the previous day. Red and white coal also eased by 1 qian. However, Jiangxi white coal remained stable. There was no fixed market price for Mack white coal yesterday, with some selling for 18 liang and others selling for 18 liang and 5 or 6 qian.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Essays

Strength 239

— Buddha

The strength of things originates from movement. Without movement, there is no way to see its strength. However, if it is seen only after movement, its strength is no longer reliable. Therefore, those who are good at using their strength can predict it before it moves.

The German scholar Rudolf Eucken said, "Modern civilization is the civilization of strength. Strength is respected to the extreme, and it is used in every possible way." These words are indeed true. Therefore, if you want to survive in a world of competition, if you want to preserve your strength, first do not waste or divide your own strength, and only then will your strength be sufficient and complete.

Considering the dynamics in physics, the thickness of its strength can be measured before it moves. However, the more it moves, the more the strength in physiology increases, and the more the strength becomes apparent. If it does not move, not only will one's own strength not be expressed, but it will also be exploited by external forces, and its strength will not be able to be preserved.

Therefore, those who want to preserve their strength must first start moving. If you cherish this strength and do not use it, you are destroying it.

The country does not love those who love romance; butterflies dance endlessly.

A defeated general receives a reward; a youth who saves the country is imprisoned.

Before throwing bombs, he sends a letter; this action will become a beautiful story for thousands of years.

The Yun family is descended from Yang Yun; they fled to Jiangnan in the past to avoid disaster.

Academics

Quartz 241

— Tao Xiaotao

You have already read and done a lot of manuscripts on physics, chemistry, and manufacturing. Now I will talk to you about minerals that are closer to people:

The sand and gravel that we usually see, the rocks on high mountains, are all made of quartz. Quartz is widely distributed and is also a mineral that we see every day. It has many uses. It can help those with nearsightedness and farsightedness see things, and it can also be used to make seals and decorations. I will introduce it below:

Quartz crystals are hexagonal prisms or hexagonal pyramids. Its texture is extremely hard and difficult to dissolve. It usually requires a very high temperature from a hydrogen-oxygen flame to dissolve it. After dissolving, it becomes a glass-like liquid, which can also be drawn into filaments to make various chemical instruments, such as flasks, funnels, crucibles, etc., as well as optical instruments such as lenses, etc. The things made are far superior to those made of glass. However, it is not easy to distinguish them from glass instruments. Generally, there are always traces of bubbles in the middle of things made of glass, but there are no traces of bubbles in the middle of things made of pure quartz. There are also methods for distinguishing hardness and specific gravity, but you have to break the object to test it. It is not dissolved by once-occurring acids, but amorphous quartz can be dissolved in hydrofluoric acid, and crystalline quartz can be dissolved in a mixed solution of hydrofluoric acid and nitric acid. It is made of a combination of oxygen and silicon. Because it contains many impurities, it is generally divided into three categories. I will describe them separately below:

(1) Crystal

Crystal is quartz with no impurities. It is colorless and transparent like glass. It is used to make optical instruments and chemical instruments. Although the things made are far superior to those made of glass, they are much more valuable. How are many colored crystals made? Those containing manganese are purple.

Those containing titanium are red. Those containing carbon are gray. This kind of crystal often grows in clusters in rocks or in mineral veins.

(2) Flint and Agate

Flint is what is commonly called firestone. It is named because it can be ignited by rubbing it. Agate is a translucent quartz with beautiful stripes. This is because it is superimposed with similar jasper, jade, etc.

(3) Opal

Opal is an opaque, non-crystalline quartz. Because it contains moisture, it is not as strong as crystal, flint, or agate. It is easily broken and is brown or milky white. Opals are polished into very good decorations.

Society Improvement Discussion Group

Points for Improvement at Banquets 242

— Ms. Ouyang Jinping

Banquets are a small matter, but there are still areas for improvement that we often overlook. I will briefly write them down for the adoption of the comrades in our discussion group.

Page 20

(1) Keep Time Strictly: Westerners value time the most. Therefore, there is a saying that "time is money." Chinese people treat the time specified on the invitation as a mere formality. We often see the host setting the time for dinner at 7:00 PM, but guests arrive at 8:00 PM or 9:00 PM, causing other guests to sit and wait, and the host to feel hungry and tired, with an unpleasant expression. This is not the way for guests and hosts to have a pleasant gathering.

(2) Eliminate Finger-Guessing Games: When guests attend a banquet, after drinking and becoming excited, they often play finger-guessing games, making loud noises and roars, as if they are crazy. This interrupts the conversations of others sitting nearby, and female guests are discouraged. This bad habit should be improved immediately. Those in the business community may talk about business conditions, and those in the academic community may discuss academic matters. Why bother with finger-guessing games?

(3) Refrain from Forcing Others to Drink: The ancient sage said, "Only wine has no limit, and excess leads to chaos." It is often seen that guests at the table use barbaric methods to force those who are not good at drinking to get drunk. After getting drunk, they may scold others indiscriminately or violently beat others, exhibiting all kinds of strange behaviors. Onlookers find this amusing. Unfortunately, if the alcohol causes an outburst, there is even a risk of blood vessels rupturing. I hope that we will eliminate this practice immediately.

(4) Should Have the Responsibility of Guiding Etiquette: When bringing children to a banquet, the elders should teach them etiquette, so that there will be no incidents of fighting for food or disturbing the order of the seats. Other things such as "do not rest your elbows when sitting side by side" and "do not mess up the bowls and chopsticks" should be guided at any time to improve the personality of the children and avoid being laughed at.

(5) Pay Attention to Signing the Invitation List: When a host throws a banquet, they always consider the number of distinguished guests listed on the invitation list to determine the number of seats to reserve. Therefore, all guests should sign "Arrived" when they arrive. If they have important matters and cannot attend, they can sign "Respectfully Decline" or "Cannot Attend," etc. It is often seen that people in society only write "Noted" on the invitation list, and the host cannot determine whether they will attend or not. Isn't this too much trouble in terms of pre-arranging the seats? Those who are invited to a banquet should pay attention to improving the small signing procedure.

A Corner of Society

A Scene of Labor-Capital Conflict 243

— Fumin

Fight! Suddenly, a series of shouts and fights erupted at the entrance of the alley. Mixed with the shouts was the sharp cursing of a woman.

Running out the door, I saw a large group of people like a tide escorting the most high-spirited XXX lawyer in our neighborhood backward.

The crowd stopped in front of the local police station. Two people twisted the lawyer into the small police rest room, and in front of the station chief, they each stated their reasons and details.

At the same time, the crowd waiting outside the door began their propaganda work. They told the visitors who were standing nearby watching,

They were tenants on XXX Road and XXX Lane in Zhabei. The rent before the war was $11.40. Because it was located in a war zone, it would inevitably suffer considerable losses after the war. After the war, the landlord repaired the house and wanted to increase the rent, jumping from $11.40 to $22. The tenants could not afford to pay the rent, so he (the lawyer) sent someone to throw away the furniture, regardless of whether there was anyone in the house. He opened the door and threw it out.

"Humph! He reduces or waives the rent for his own house, but increases the rent for other people's houses. How can this be!" A fat woman said, spraying saliva as she put her hands on her hips.

"We must teach him to publish a statement in the newspaper!" A fat man with a bare chest and a protruding belly said, clenching his fists and raising his arms.

"Damn it! Right or wrong, don't beat him up first and then talk," a friend wearing a straw hat said, rubbing his hands together.

Because the matter was serious, the station chief could not resolve it, so it was sent to the head office. The negotiators came out. Four more policemen were added next to the lawyer. When they walked to the place where the lawyer lived, the lawyer drilled inside and went home. The crowd wanted to chase after him and grab him, but they were stopped by the gatekeeper. So there was a reaction.

Charge! With a shout, the people in the back pushed the people in the front. The people in the front were afraid of getting beaten, so they turned around and drilled into the crowd. Four policemen ran over and suppressed them.

After a while, the lawyer came out in a car. The gatekeeper took the lead and opened the way with a rattan cane in front of the car, scaring the crowd from daring to step forward to stop him. At the same time, many people supported him beside the car. These people, on the surface, looked like idlers, but in reality, they were all his subordinates. With great difficulty, they cleared a path, and the car sped out of the alley toward the head office. Afterwards, the crowd also flocked away.

Later, I heard that 21 tenants were arrested, but the lawyer came out without any problems.

School Scene

So That's How It Is 244

— Xiu Ye

Recently, I came back from school and suddenly saw a group of slender ladies in long cheongsams and high heels in our alley, in addition to a few familiar faces. I asked my family and learned that a XX Girls' Normal School had recently moved into our alley, and these owners of long cheongsams and high heels were high-achieving students of the school.

I have often heard the name XX Girls' Normal School since I was a primary school student ten years ago. No, it would be better to say that I have seen it, because at the beginning of each semester, two of their enrollment advertisements will definitely appear on the wall of our alley in addition to the [Yao Zuodun] [Double Magpie] and other recruitment papers; sometimes, our door cracks will also be filled with flyers introducing X people ... tuition fees are reduced by half to show preferential treatment. I heard that there are two to three hundred students now. Don't you have a big sign in our alley? My family told me, really, the big sign at the entrance of the alley is so big that it can cover the three words XX Lane, the name of our alley.

This school occupies the first and second houses at the entrance of our alley: its gate faces the road, and its body is an alley house, so this school can be regarded as being between a road school and an alley school. Although the house is not big, in addition to being used as classrooms and female teachers' bedrooms, it also has a girls' dormitory, but only for older students, probably because small students require a lot of manpower to take care of.

When I walked past their door at night, I often saw a few young girls laughing and talking at the door. At the same time, on the steps opposite, there were often young men wearing Western-style trousers and cloth gowns walking back and forth. Yesterday evening, when I came back from the cinema, I suddenly saw a group of people gathered at the entrance of our alley, not far from my home. Probably some Miss has committed suicide or the boss's wife has run away in the alley again, I thought silently, and at the same time quickened my pace.

As I got closer, I could see clearly that the people were all gathered at the door of the school. The door of the school was wide open, and many people were squeezing in and out. Following the sight of the crowd, I found a new sign on that big sign. The snow-bright gold letter sign has an attached XX Night School XX Specialized Course. Old Wang, who wears a red cheongsam and an apple-shaped face, also lives there, otherwise who would be happy to put on eight outfits and walk there every night, arriving a quarter of an hour early before class, just when they have eaten dinner, slowly attacking, enjoying it, a young man wearing four hundred degrees of myopia glasses was telling his companion in the crowd. I took a closer look, and it turned out that a few comrades who had been wandering on the steps opposite were all present here, each holding an application form in their hands.

Oh, so that's how it is.

Behind the Scenes

Impersonating a Friend 245

— Dai'er

Yesterday, a man in a Western suit, about 40 years old, came to a certain family and asked to see the male owner. The servant replied that he was not at home, so he asked for paper and a pen, and wrote a note with the name of a certain person in a certain room of a certain hotel. As he was about to leave, he stopped again.

He asked to see the hostess. The servant took the note and reported it to the hostess. The hostess thought it was an important matter, so she came downstairs to meet him. The man in the Western suit immediately called her "Teacher's Wife" and said that he needed four yuan to send a telegram and asked to borrow it. The woman saw that he was a stranger and was very surprised, but since he was a friend of her husband, she should lend it to him, so she took out a five-yuan bill and gave it to him. He thanked her and left, saying that he would return it at six o'clock that evening.

When six o'clock came, the person did not appear, and she began to feel suspicious. When her husband returned home, he did not recognize having such a friend. She realized that she had been deceived. At this time, not only was the money lost, but she also received nagging complaints from her husband. She regretted it endlessly.

Prank

A Doctor's Prank 246

— Yongxiang

Mrs. Zhang and Mrs. Wang were both uneducated people who liked to talk nonsense. They often made waves out of nothing. One day, Mrs. Zhang had a slight illness and asked Mrs. Wang to accompany her to see Dr. □ on □□ Road.

They talked and laughed all the way. When they arrived at the doctor's office, they registered. When the doctor was taking her pulse on her hand, they started talking loudly again for no reason. How many feet long should the cheongsam be! How many inches high should the collar be……………How beautiful it is! They were talking with relish, forgetting that they had come to see a doctor.

Hey! The prescription is ready, go and get it, the doctor said impatiently.

They were shocked by this shout and stopped talking. They hurriedly took the prescription to □ Pharmacy to buy medicine.

Hey! Sir, buy a dose of medicine, Mrs. Zhang said.

The pharmacy clerk took the prescription and looked at it. He said with a vivid expression, don't make a mistake, this is a pharmacy.

Sir, that's right! I'm here to buy medicine, Mrs. Zhang said in a questioning tone.

This paper is written with clothing sizes, not a prescription, the pharmacy clerk said with a frown.

Huh! Strange! Mrs. Zhang said in a daze.

Doctor, I asked you to see a doctor and prescribe medicine, why are you writing clothing sizes? Don't make fun of me, Mrs. Zhang said with slight anger and annoyance.

What were you talking about when you were seeing the doctor, the doctor said with a smile.

Later, they realized their mistake and begged the doctor to rewrite the prescription and went to buy medicine.

▲Civil Judgments: The case of Wei Lianji, i.e. Xia Wei, against Shen Renxinghao for deposit (main text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 51 taels of standard silver and interest at a rate of 7% per month from the date of deposit until the date of the end of execution. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.▲The case of Zhu Hongru of Daxing Real Estate Company against Shen Shaogang of Youcheng Company for rent arrears (main text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 9,620 yuan, 1 jiao, and 3 fen of foreign currency, and statutory late payment interest at a rate of 5% per annum from the time of the lawsuit until the time of the end of execution. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.▲The case of Wang Chengzhai against Sun Minxian for cohabitation (main text) The defendant shall send the plaintiff's daughter, Yueqin, and the plaintiff's son, Zhongfa, back to Shanghai to cohabit with the plaintiff. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.▲The case of Taili Company against Wang Jiatong for rent (main text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 122 yuan and 4 jiao of foreign currency for rent. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.▲The case of Xie Yibin against Chen Zhusan for bill payment (main text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 3,000 taels of silver, and agreed late payment interest at a rate of 12 taels per thousand per month from August 25, 1931 until the date of the end of execution. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.▲The case of Shi Dalasheng against Zhu Shizhen for debt (main text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 150 yuan of foreign currency for debt, and the repayment shall be evenly distributed over twelve months from the date of the judgment's determination. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.▲The case of Yao Fayun against Zou Haishan and others for goods (main text) The defendants Zou Haishan and Zou Gongrang shall repay the plaintiff 582 taels and 8 mace and 5 fen of silver. The defendant Wu Mian Zhao shall repay the plaintiff 90 yuan of foreign currency. The defendants shall bear the litigation costs in proportion.▲The case of Mei Fu Hang against Du Hebao for goods (main text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 867 yuan, 3 jiao, and 6 fen of foreign currency for goods, and late payment interest calculated at a rate of 5% per annum from the date of the lawsuit until the date of full repayment. Provisional execution is permitted in this case. If the defendant deposits the aforementioned amount or secures a reliable shop as security for the aforementioned amount, provisional execution shall be waived. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.▲The appeal case of Xu Jundao against Bi Jichun for rent (main text) The appeal and incidental appeal are both rejected. The appellant shall bear the costs of the second instance litigation.▲The case of Taichang Company against Ma Dunhetang’s Master Ma Youzhi and others for rent and eviction (main text) The defendant Ma Dunhetang’s Master Ma Youzhi shall repay the plaintiff 210 yuan of silver and 36 jiao of small money for rent. If his property is insufficient to pay the debt, the defendant Dunhetang shall be responsible for the repayment. The defendant Tianchenghao shall repay the plaintiff 175 yuan of silver and 30 jiao of small money for rent on behalf of the defendant Zhang Shunxing. Provisional execution is permitted in this case. If the defendants Ma Dunhetang’s Master Ma Youzhi and Tianchenghao secure reliable shops as security for the aforementioned amounts separately, provisional execution shall be waived. The remaining claims are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff, excluding the part concerning Zhang Shunxing, and the remaining part shall be borne by the defendant Ma Dunhetang’s Master Ma Youzhi for two-fifths, and by the defendants Tianchenghao and Dunhetang and the plaintiff for one-fifth each.▲The case of Ni Yangzhou and others against Xu Xiangbo and others for goods (main text) The defendant Cai Songnian shall repay the plaintiff Ni Yangzhou 340 yuan of foreign currency for goods, and repay the plaintiff Zheng Fangrui 325 yuan, 8 jiao, and 5 fen of foreign currency for goods. The remaining claims are rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne equally by the plaintiffs Ni Yangzhou and Zheng Fangrui, excluding the part concerning the defendant Xu Xiangbo, and the remaining part shall be borne by the defendant Cai Songnian.▲The case of Pudong Bank against Tianshengfu Silk and Cotton Cloth Shop for debt (main text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 2,200 taels of silver and late payment interest calculated according to the bank's overdue interest rate from June 1, 1932 until the date of the end of execution. The defendant shall bear the litigation costs.▲The case of Sachs against Xu Xiangyou and others for rent arrears (main text) The defendant Xu Xiangyou shall repay the plaintiff 319 yuan of foreign currency. Xu Huisheng shall repay 396 yuan. Zhu Ziyong shall repay 408 yuan. Wang Shunji shall repay 140 yuan. Xin Da shall repay 264 yuan. Zhang A Ming and Gong Wang each shall repay 330 yuan. The defendants shall bear one-tenth of the litigation costs in proportion.▲The case of Banque de l'Indochine against Wu Yuntai and others for bills (main text) Wu Yuntai shall repay the plaintiff 9,773 francs. Wu Shenyou and Yang Ye Qiao each shall repay the plaintiff 488.065 francs, and interest at a rate of 5% per annum from April 17, 1931 until the date of the end of execution. The remaining claims of the plaintiff are rejected. The plaintiff shall bear twelve-thirteenths of the litigation costs, and the remaining part shall be borne by the defendants in proportion.

▲Civil Instructions: Zhu Zuoting's request for provisional attachment for Dan Yunzhang The court finds that the ruling requires Dan Yunzhang to provide cash or equivalent securities and does not require a shop guarantee. The request to provide a guarantee is inconsistent with the ruling and should not be discussed.▲Du Yuesheng's request for the return of account books for the case of suing Shen Fuji and others for goods. The court understands from the petition that the judgment in this case has not yet been determined, and it is not appropriate to return the account books in advance.▲Chen Jisheng, manager of Eldred Company, and Zhang Xiangji's request for cancellation of the case and return of silver dollars for rent arrears. The court understands from the petition that the cancellation should be approved and you should come to the court at 9:00 am on September 6 this year to receive the money.▲Bao Jiashan and Xu Zhangyuan's request for correction of the eviction order. The court understands from the petition that the request should be approved and the execution order can be corrected to open the address as stated.▲Jiang Jisheng and Yuanheng Copper and Iron Bed Shop's request for execution for rent arrears. The court understands from the petition that the summons should be ordered to pursue.▲Chen Shaozhong and Tang Dongsheng's request for the unsealing and cancellation of the certificate case. The court understands from the petition that since the case has been settled out of court, the unsealing and cancellation should be approved.▲Feng Haifu and Yuanshenghao's request for installment payment for the bill case. The court understands from the petition that the debtor has been overdue for a long time and should wait for compulsory execution. The request for installment payment should not be discussed. (Above September 1)
